前瞻性临床试验

105项研究。疾病场景：LBCL/HGBL 73项、SCNSL/CNS复发或预防 13项、PMBCL/特殊亚型 9项、转化/Richter 7项；药物/技术：CAR-T/细胞治疗 38项、BTKi 17项、化疗/免疫化疗 14项、其他/未明确药物 14项。

001DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S286

cd19/cd22双特异性car-t细胞治疗复发/难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤及其机制研究：一项前瞻性、单臂、单中心、2期临床试验

cd19/cd22 bispecific car-t cell therapy for relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma and mechanistic investigation: a prospective, single-arm, single-center, phase 2 clinical trial

P 患者群体

B细胞非霍奇金淋巴瘤；大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=73；治疗线数/场景：二线，三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：CD19/CD22靶向CAR-T(同仁医院)；靶点：CD19，CD22；类别：CAR-T，自体细胞，经基因修饰；分组：试验组：CAR2219

C 对照措施

002DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S284

cd19car t细胞扩增过程中支链氨基酸的生物利用度与lbcl中有利的t细胞状态和临床反应有关

branched-chain amino acid bioavailability during cd19 car t-cell expansion associates with favorable t-cell states and clinical response in lbcl

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=66

I 干预措施

003DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S236

vispa-cel，一种pd-1敲除的异基因抗cd19car-t细胞疗法，用于复发/难治性b细胞非霍奇金淋巴瘤患者（鹿角1期临床试验）

vispa-cel, an allogeneic anti-cd19 car-t cell therapy with a pd-1 knockout, in patients with relapsed/refractory b cell non-hodgkin lymphoma (antler phase 1 clinical trial)

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=84；治疗线数/场景：三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：Vispacabtagene regedleucel；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，异体细胞，腺相关病毒载体AAV，经基因修饰，CRISPR/Cas9；分组：所有患者均接受淋巴细胞清除化疗（环磷酰胺+氟达拉滨）后输注vispa-cel，剂量分为40×10^6、80×10^6、120×10^6三个水平；推荐剂量（RP2D）为80×10^6，并设有2L LBCL确认队列（80×10^6）

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：所有患者均接受淋巴细胞清除化疗（环磷酰胺+氟达拉滨）后输注vispa-cel，剂量分为40×10^6、80×10^6、120×10^6三个水平；推荐剂量（RP2D）为80×10^6，并设有2L LBCL确认队列（80×10^6）

O 结局指标

1. 总有效率（ORR）：82%（确认队列） 2. 完全缓解率（CR）：64%（确认队列） 3. 中位无进展生存期（PFS）和缓解持续时间（DOR）：未达到 4. 12个月PFS率：51% 5. 安全性：CRS发生率55%（≥3级1%），ICANS发生率14%（≥3级4%），感染发生率51%（≥3级25%），≥3级持续血细胞减少28%，IEC-HS发生率2%（均≥3级）；5例死亡（1例相关，1例可能相关，3例无关）

004DLBCL/LBCL前瞻性临床试验LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S235

epcore dlbcl-1的结果：epcoritamab（epcor）与研究者选择的化学免疫疗法（cit）在复发/难治性大b细胞淋巴瘤（r/r lbcl）患者中的随机3期研究

results from epcore dlbcl-1: randomized phase 3 study of epcoritamab (epcor) vs investigator’s choice chemoimmunotherapy (cit) in patients with relapsed/refractory large b-cell lymphoma (r/r lbcl)

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=483；治疗线数/场景：二线，三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：艾可瑞妥单抗；靶点：CD20，CD3；类别：双特异性抗体；分组：试验组：Epcoritamab单药治疗；对照组：研究者选择的化学免疫治疗（包括R-GemOx和BR）

C 对照措施

对照/比较：试验组：Epcoritamab单药治疗|||对照组：研究者选择的化学免疫治疗（包括R-GemOx和BR）

O 结局指标

主要终点PFS：HR 0.74 (95% CI 0.60-0.92; P=0.0059)，24个月PFS率：30% vs 13%|||关键次要终点OS：HR 0.83 (95% CI 0.67-1.04; P=0.1003)（未达到统计学显著性）|||完全缓解率(CRR)：38% vs 26% (名义P=0.0032)|||缓解持续时间(DOR)中位数：37个月 vs 6个月|||完全缓解持续时间(DOCR)中位数：未达到 vs 11个月|||至下次治疗时间(TTNT)中位数：7个月 vs 4个月 (名义P<0.0001)|||安全性：Epcor组3-4级感染30% vs 12%；5级TEAE 17% vs 6%；CRS 53%（3级3%）；ICANS 4%（3-4级1%）

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: 483 pts (epcor 241; CIT 242 [R-GemOx 174; BR 68]) were randomized; 67% were randomized in 2022 or later, coinciding with the COVID-19 Omicron period. Median follow-up was 43.2 mo (epcor) and 42.3 mo (CIT). Median age was 71 y (range, 28–89); 53% of pts were from North America/Western Europe; 73% had ≥ 2 pLOT, and 34% had ≥ 3 pLOT; 69% were refractory to last line of treatment (tx); 15% had prior SCT, and 11% had prior CAR-T. \n A statistically significant improvement in PFS was demonstrated with epcor vs CIT (HR, 0.74 [95% CI, 0.60–0.92]; P =0.0059; 24-mo PFS: 30% vs 13%). Furthermore, clinically meaningful higher complete response rate (CRR: 38% vs 26%; nominal P value 0.0032), longer durability of response (median DOR 37 vs 6 mo; DOCR NR vs 11 mo) and longer TTNT (7 vs 4 mo; nominal P value \n Mean tx duration was longer for epcor vs CIT (11 vs 2 mo); 31% of pts received ≥ 12 cycles of epcor. Higher rates of grade 3–4 infections (30% vs 12%) and any-grade COVID-19 (36% vs 11%) were reported in the epcor arm; exposure-adjusted event rates were 4.3 vs 4.9 (grade 3–4 infections) and 4.4 vs 3.4 (any-grade COVID-19) per 100 pt-mo. Grade 5 TEAEs occurred in 17% vs 6% (exposure-adjusted, 1.5 vs 1.8 per 100 pt-mo) and were largely attributable to grade 5 COVID-19 (9% vs 2%). CRS was reported in 53% (grade 3, 3%) in the epcor arm and ICANS in 4% (grade 3–4, 1%). Summary/Conclusion: EPCORE DLBCL-1 is the largest randomized phase 3 trial in R/R LBCL and the first to demonstrate a statistically significant improvement in PFS with a CD3×CD20 bsAb monotherapy vs combination CIT. Furthermore, compared with CIT, epcor resulted in clinically meaningful improvements in CRR, DOR, DOCR, and less frequent use of subsequent tx, demonstrating deep and durable responses. OS was not significantly different, being confounded by COVID-19 mortality and use of novel subsequent tx. Observed AEs were consistent with the established epcor safety profile and the expected profile for a CD3×CD20 bsAb.

为避免误读，改用EHA页面原文结果；需人工翻译后再对外使用。

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: The median age of the final cohort was 57 years; 41% were female, and patients had received a median of two prior lines of therapy. At baseline, 401 trackable somatic mutations were identified for MRD monitoring (mean: 6 per patient). The most frequently mutated genes were TP53 (44%), CREBBP (30%), KMT2D (24%), IGLL5 (22%), and BCL2 (20%). Early MRD assessment (day +7/+14) identified patients at increased risk of progression, with ctDNA positivity demonstrating significant prognostic impact (one-year PFS: 23% vs 100%; HR, 10; 95% CI, 1.37–72.48; p=0.02), indicating that molecular kinetics precede conventional imaging (Figure A). At day +30, ctDNA MRD positivity retained independent prognostic value (HR 4.5, 95% CI 1.03–19.37; p=0.02), comparable to PET/CT (HR 8.3, 95% CI 4.41–15.6; p Summary/Conclusion: Tumor-informed ctDNA monitoring enables very early risk stratification after CAR-T therapy in LBCL, identifying high-risk patients within the first two weeks post-infusion, before radiologic assessment. At day +30, ctDNA MRD positivity shows strong prognostic value, and integration of molecular and metabolic response improves outcome discrimination. ctDNA analysis is particularly useful when PET findings generate uncertainty, clarifying disease status. These results support incorporating longitudinal ctDNA monitoring into prospective CAR-T trials to enable earlier, biology-driven, risk-adapted strategies.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: As of July 15, 2025, 14 patients underwent leukapheresis and 12 received relma-cel. The median age was 61.5 years (range, 46–76; 41.7% ≥65 years), and 58.3% were male. High-risk disease features were common: 50.0% had an International Prognostic Index ≥3, 83.3% had Ann Arbor stage III/IV disease, 41.7% had elevated baseline lactate dehydrogenase, and 83.3% had the non-germinal center B-cell-like subtype. Prior therapies included ≥3 lines in 41.7% of patients; 25.0% had received polatuzumab vedotin and 25.0% had received CD3/CD20 bispecific antibodies (one patient was primary refractoriness, two patients were relapsed within 12 months of first-line therapy, and three patients were subsequently treated with bispecific antibodies, and all were refractory to bispecific antibody). Overall, 33.3% had relapsed disease, 66.7% were refractory to their most recent therapy. 41.7% of patients received bridging therapy. With a median follow-up was 4.6 months (range, 2.79–5.85), in the modified intent to treatment (mITT) population (n=12), the investigator-assessed ORR at 3 months was 58.33%, with a CRR of 41.67%, meeting the primary endpoint. The best investigator-assessed ORR was 66.67%, with a best CRR of 41.67%. Independent review committee (IRC)-assessed ORR at 3 months was 58.33%, with a CRR of 58.33%. The best ORR was 75.00%, with a best CRR of 58.33% ( Figure 1 ). Three patients refractory to bispecific antibodies achieved PR, PD and CR, respectively, at 1 month; excluding the patient with PD, the other two patients had PD and CR respectively at 3 months. Median DOR, PFS, and OS have not been reached. Relma-cel manufactured with JWLV011 demonstrated a manageable safety profile with no treatment-related deaths, or study discontinuations due to adverse events. All patients experienced treatment-related adverse events, 8.3% developed serious treatment-emergent adverse events. Cytokine release syndrome occurred in 83.3% of patients, all grade 1-2. No patient developed neurological toxicities. Summary/Conclusion: Relma-cel manufactured using the domestically produced lentiviral vector demonstrated favorable efficacy and a manageable safety profile in adult patients with R/R LBCL. These findings support the feasibility of in-house lentiviral vector manufacturing without compromising clinical performance.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 338 pt charts (US: 168 [49.7%]; EU: 170 [50.3%]) were abstracted by 145 physicians (US: 73 [50.3%]; EU: 72 [49.7%]). Pts were 66.0% male with median (IQR) age 61.5 (55.1, 67.4) years at CAR-T infusion, 51.2% had double/triple-hit disease, 72.8% were primary refractory, and 53.0% had revised International Prognostic Index score ≥3. \n Most pts received axicabtagene ciloleucel (65.1%), followed by lisocabtagene maraleucel (21.9%) and tisagenlecleucel (13.0%) CAR-T. Median (IQR) time from the last tafa dose until CAR-T was 1.2 (0.6-2.3) months; follow-up time post CAR-T was 7.4 (3.3-10.6) months; and 73.1% were still alive at the time of last contact. \n Overall, ORR for CAR-T was 81.1%, and grade ≥3 (severe) CRS and ICANS occurred in 7.4% and 3.8% of pts, respectively. ORR by CAR-T line and the observed tafa/CAR-T treatment sequences are reported in the Table. CRS and ICANS by CAR-T line are reported in the Figure . \n Table. Summary/Conclusion: This large, global, real-world study shows that prior exposure to tafa does not appear to adversely affect the effectiveness nor safety of subsequent CAR-T therapy in patients with R/R DLBCL. These results are particularly relevant with recent phase 3 data for tafa in the front‑line setting of DLBCL. While these real-world study findings should be interpreted in the context of an observational cohort, they support tafa followed by CAR-T therapy as a feasible and potentially favorable sequencing strategy.

kite-753治疗复发/难治性b细胞淋巴瘤患者的1期研究：最新的安全性和疗效结果

a phase 1 study of kite-753 in patients (pts) with relapsed/refractory (r/r) b-cell lymphoma: updated safety and efficacy results

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤，非霍奇金淋巴瘤；N=33；治疗线数/场景：三线，末线

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：KITE-753；靶点：CD19，CD20；类别：CAR-T，自体细胞，经基因修饰；分组：试验组1：KITE-753 (0.3×10^5 CAR T cells/kg)；试验组2：KITE-753 (1×10^5 CAR T cells/kg)；试验组3：KITE-753 (2×10^5 CAR T cells/kg)

C 对照措施

多组/多方案比较：试验组1：KITE-753 (0.3×10^5 CAR T cells/kg)；试验组2：KITE-753 (1×10^5 CAR T cells/kg)；试验组3：KITE-753 (2×10^5 CAR T cells/kg)

O 结局指标

总体反应率（ORR）在CAR-naive患者最高剂量组（DL3，n=17）为88%；完全缓解率（CR）在数据截止时71%，数据截止后76%（1例从PR转为CR）；在既往接受过CAR-T治疗的患者（所有剂量水平，n=10）中，3例（30%）达CR，2例（20%）达PR；任何级别CRS：24%为1级，24%为2级，3%为3级，无4/5级；任何级别ICANS：2例1级，4例2级，无≥3级；中位CRS发生时间6.0天，中位持续时间6.0天；中位ICANS发生时间10.5天，中位持续时间3.5天；5例死亡（2例与KITE-753无关的感染，3例疾病进展）；与axi-cel相比，KITE-753的神经毒性相关细胞因子IL-15水平更低，CAR-T细胞扩增峰值延迟

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: As of 12/03/25, 33 pts received KITE-753 (3 in DL 1, 8 in DL 2, 22 in DL 3). Median follow-up was 7.4 months (range, 5.8-12.7). Median age at analysis was 59.0 years (range, 25-84); 88% of pts had LBCL and 12% had indolent non-Hodgkin lymphoma, and 76% had Stage III/IV disease. Nine pts (27% of all; 31% of LBCL) were primary refractory and 10 (30%) had received prior CAR T-cell therapy. No DLTs occurred in dose escalation. Grade ≥3 adverse events occurred in 85% of pts (91% in DL 3), primarily cytopenias. Eight pts (24%) had max Grade 1 CRS, 8 (24%) had max Grade 2 CRS, 1 had max Grade 3 CRS (LBCL, DL 2), and none had Grade 4/5 CRS. Median time to CRS onset was 6.0 days; median duration was 6.0 days. Two pts had Grade 1 ICANS (1 each in DL 2 and DL 3), 4 had Grade 2 ICANS (1 in DL 2, 3 in DL 3), and none had Grade ≥3 ICANS. Median time to ICANS onset was 10.5 days; median duration was 3.5 days. Five pts died: 2 due to infections unrelated to KITE-753 per investigator assessment and 3 due to progression. ORR in CAR-naive pts at DL 3 (n=17) was 88%; CR rate was 71% (12/17) at the data cutoff and 76% (13/17) post-data cutoff, with 1 pt converting from a partial response (PR) to a CR. In pts with prior CAR exposure (all DLs; n=10), 3 (30%) had a CR and 2 (20%) had a PR. In a comparative analysis of KITE-753 vs axicabtagene ciloleucel (axi-cel; ZUMA-1), levels of the neurotoxicity-associated cytokine, IL-15, were lower with KITE-753, coinciding with an improved toxicity profile. Peak CAR T-cell expansion was delayed with KITE-753 vs axi-cel; IL-2, INF-γ, and granzyme B kinetics correlated with delayed time to peak. These favorable pharmacokinetic and pharmacodynamic profiles may reflect KITE-753’s optimized CAR T-cell dose that mitigates toxicity and its rapid manufacturing process that preserves CAR T-cell fitness. Summary/Conclusion: KITE-753, with a unique CAR design and rapid manufacturing process preserving a naive T-cell phenotype, at the highest DL showed high CR rates in CAR-naive pts and a favorable safety profile with only low-grade CRS and ICANS.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 317 patients were included in the analysis: 165 (52%) received glofit and 152 (48%) epco. At BsAb initiation, median age was 70 years (range, 22-93), 13% had double-hit LBCL, 69% had an international prognostic index score of ≥3, median prior lines of therapy (LOT) was 3 (range, 1-9), and median ALC was 0.6×10³/µL (IQR, 0.3-1.0; range, 0-39.1×10³/µL). Any-grade CRS and ICANS occurred in 112 (36%) and 37 (12%) of patients, respectively, with grade ≥3 occurring in 13 (4%) and 6 (2%). Overall response rates (ORR) and complete response rates (CR) were 51% and 34%, respectively. After a median follow-up of 12.1 months, median PFS was 3.9 months. The optimal ALC threshold in the training dataset was 0.25×10³/µL. In the overall cohort, 260 patients (82%) had high ALC. Compared to the low pre-treatment ALC ( Summary/Conclusion: An optimal ALC threshold of 0.25×10³/µL could identify patients with R/R LBCL who may experience deeper responses and longer PFS with BsAb. Biological analysis, aimed at investigating clinically relevant T-cell subgroups, and prospective validation of these findings are warranted.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: High baseline CD20 expression (> 80% positive tumor cells) was observed in 89% (319/357) of biomarker-evaluable biopsies from patients with DLBCL and FL; CD20 expression 10% (PR, n = 3; SD, n = 2; PD, n = 18); patients with CR were excluded due to no detectable tumor at C2D15, limiting generalizability. CD20 expression was maintained on tx in 4 of 5 patients with PR/SD. CD20 expression MS4A1 mutations in the extracellular and transmembrane domains; transcriptional downregulation was observed in 2 (17%) patients. Notably, 1 patient with SD who maintained CD20 expression at C2D15 harbored a pre-existing missense mutation in extracellular loop 2 that may have interfered with epcor binding. Of the 18 pts with PD, 7 maintained CD20 expression, of whom 4 showed on-tx and EOT reductions in intratumoral CD3 T cells. Summary/Conclusion: Whilst most patients with DLBCL and FL have high baseline CD20 expression and high response rates to epcor, clinical responses were also observed in some patients with baseline CD20 expression MS4A1 mutations and transcriptional downregulation in a subset of patients. Decreased intratumoral T-cell numbers were also identified as a potential mechanism of resistance. Similar changes in CD20 expression at progression have been reported with other CD3xCD20 bispecific antibodies, suggesting antigen modulation may contribute to resistance in some patients. These findings support further exploration of strategies to overcome antigen escape and restore therapeutic sensitivity.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: As of May 1, 2025, among TMTV-evaluable pts (n=246), high baseline TMTV (≥125cm 3 , median) was prognostic for inferior PFS (hazard ratio [HR], 1.49, p=0.004). Glofit-GemOx showed improved PFS over R-GemOx irrespective of TMTV burden (high TMTV: HR, 0.37, p \n Longitudinal ctDNA analyses showed higher rates of undetected ctDNA with Glofit-GemOx vs R-GemOx across all timepoints: 47.7% vs 9.5% at Days 25–65 (early treatment), 65.6% vs 32.1% at Days 65–110 (mid-treatment), and 70.0% vs 31.6% at Days 110–220 ( Figure ). Among pts treated with Glofit-GemOx, undetected ctDNA status at Cycle 3 was strongly associated with prolonged PFS (p Summary/Conclusion: These results demonstrate the potential for TMTV and ctDNA as powerful prognostic tools in R/R DLBCL. Glofit-GemOx demonstrated superior efficacy over R-GemOx regardless of tumor burden (TMTV or ctDNA). In addition, longitudinal ctDNA monitoring supports early response assessment, with undetected ctDNA status by Cycle 3 emerging as a strong predictor of long-term PFS. Higher rates of undetectable ctDNA were observed with Glofit-GemOx vs R-GemOx, validating its clinical benefit and supporting the superior efficacy observed in the primary analysis of STARGLO.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: By February 2026, 39 patients with a median age of 78.0 years (IQR: 75.0–84.0) were evaluable, including 43.6% (n=17) aged ≥80. High-risk features were prevalent: 69.2% each presented with an IPI score of 3–5, stage III–IV disease, or elevated LDH. Histologically, 97.4% had DLBCL, and one (2.6%) had primary cutaneous DLBCL, leg type (PCDLBCL, LT); 77.0% were of the non-GCB/ABC subtype. Comorbidities affected 74.3% (29/39) of this ultra-elderly cohort, most commonly cardiovascular diseases (41.0%), hypertension (35.9%), diabetes (15.4%), cerebrovascular diseases (15.4%), and prostatic hypertrophy (5.1%). \n At the data cutoff, of the 39 enrolled patients, 29 have completed the interim efficacy assessment, the CR rate was 58.6% (17/29), with an ORR of 96.5%. Among these, 37.9% (11/29) achieved a partial response, while 3.4% (1/29) experienced disease progression. Notably, in the 12 patients identified with the MCD subtype, the ORR rate was 100% (12/12), the CR rate was 66.7% (8/12). At the completion of combination therapy (C6-response), the CR rate was 91.7% (22/24), the ORR rate was 95.8 % (23/24). With a median follow-up of 7.0 months (range, 0.4–21.5), neither the median progression-free survival (PFS) nor the median overall survival (OS) has been reached. The estimated 9-month PFS rate was 92.8%. Subgroup analysis of patients aged ≥80 years (n=17) demonstrated survival outcomes comparable to the overall cohort, suggesting the sustained benefit of the chemo-free PRO regimen in the oldest-old. \n The PRO regimen demonstrated a manageable safety profile in this ultra-elderly and frail population. Grade 3-4 adverse events (AEs) were primarily pulmonary infections (17.9%) and neutropenia (10.3%). Most other hematological and non-hematological toxicities were confined to Grade 1-2 and were clinically manageable with supportive care. Summary/Conclusion: In summary, despite a high comorbidity burden (74.3%), updated data from 39 patients indicate that the chemotherapy-free PRO regimen is an effective and tolerable frontline option for elderly and frail DLBCL patients. It achieved a 91.7% CR rate at treatment completion and an estimated 9-month PFS of 92.8%, with 100% ORR in the MCD subtype. These results support PRO as a feasible strategy for vulnerable patients, including those ≥80 years who are unfit for intensive immunochemotherapy.

Results: Between August 2022 and February 2026 , a total of 45 patients were enrolled , with a median age of 59 years (range, 26-79). T he majority o f patients (9 7 . 8 %) presented with stage III-IV disease, and 4 2.2 % were over 60 years. Additionally, 68.9% of patients presented with two or more extranodal involvement , and 5 1.1 % had elevated lactate dehydrogenase levels . The double expression of MYC and BCL2 was detected in 20.0 % of patients . The median follow-up period was 21.0 months (95% CI: 16.1 - 25.9), with 42 patients being evaluable for response. The median PFS, DFS and OS have not yet been reached. The majority of adverse events (AEs) were of grade 1-2. Grade 3-4 AEs included neutropenia (71.1%), leukopenia (60.0%), decreased lymphocyte count (31.1%), and thrombocytopenia (26.7%). All AEs were effectively managed with supportive care and subsequently resolved. \n Table 1: Baseline Characteristics of the Study Population. \n \n \n \n \n Baseline characteristics Summary/Conclusion: The combination of selinexor with the R-CHOP as a first-line treatment for high-risk (IPI 3-5) GCB-DLBCL demonstrates encouraging efficacy and and a manageable safety profile.

profiling the csf-ctdna mutational landscape in a large cohort of dlbcl: implications for predicting cns relapse and clinical outcomes

P 患者群体

弥漫性大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=410

I 干预措施

前瞻性临床研究结果：profiling the csf-ctdna mutational landscape in a large cohort of dlbcl: implications for predicting cns relapse and clinical outcomes

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

CSF-ctDNA阳性率：23.9%（98/410）|||CSF(+)患者中前10个最常突变基因：MYD88 35.8%, PIM1 34.6%, CD79B 28.8%, KMT2D 24.2%, BTG2 23.3%, TP53 23.3%, H1-4 23.3%, BTG1 22.1%, BCL6 20.8%, ETV6 19.6%|||CSF(+)与初始治疗反应较差及生存较差显著相关|||CSF-ctDNA(+)对CNS复发的预测能力优于高风险的CNS-IPI评分

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Of the 410 ND-DLBCL patients, 98 (23.9%) were identified as CSF(+), among which 63 (64.3%) fulfilled both criteria, while 17 (17.3%) only met criterion 1 and 18 (18.4%) only met criterion 2 ( Figure 1B ). Among the 80 CSF(+) patients with matched tissue, plasma and CSF samples, the top 10 frequently mutated genes were MYD88 (35.8%), PIM1 (34.6%), CD79B (28.8%), KMT2D (24.2%), BTG2 (23.3%), TP53 (23.3%), H1-4 (23.3%), BTG1 (22.1%), BCL6 (20.8%) and ETV6 (19.6%) ( Figure 1C ). The mean variant allele frequency was significantly lower in CSF than in tissue and plasma samples ( Figure 1D ). As to genetic subtypes, CSF(+) patients were mostly distributed in MCD (N=37), Other (N=29), ST2 (N=10), BN2 (N=8) and TP53-disrupted subtypes (N=7), while TP53-disrupted (36.8%) and MCD (34.3%) subtypes showed highest CSF(+) ratio ( Figure 1E ). However, no difference in CSF-ctDNA burden was observed across genetic subtypes ( Figure 1F ). Furthermore, CSF(+) patients exhibited higher plasma ctDNA burden ( Figure 1G ). Patients with MCD subtype, non-GCB orign, specific extranodal sites involvement (reproductive system, kidney/adrenal gland, bone marrow) and higher IPI score were correlated with higher CSF(+) rate, while gastrointestinal tract involvement seemed negatively associated with CSF(+) ( Figure 1H ). In plasma samples, MYD88, CD79B, ETV6, IGLL5, CDKN2A, CARD11, CD274 mutations were associated with higher CSF(+) rate ( Figure 1I ), while in tissue samples, CARD11, PRDM1, MCL1 mutations seemed correlated with higher CSF(+) rate ( Figure 1J ). In RNA level, the dysregulated genes of CSF(+) patients were enriched in cytokine-cytokine receptor interaction, focal adhesion, cytoskeleton, and PI3K-AKT signaling pathways, potentially promoting CNSi in ND-DLBCL ( Figure 1K ). Moreover, CSF(+) significantly correlated with inferior response to initial treatment and worse survival in ND-DLBCL patients ( Figure 1L-1N ). Besides, CSF-ctDNA(+) demonstrated superior prediction capability for CNS relapse compared with high-risk CNS-IPI in ND-DLBCL ( Figure 1O ). Summary/Conclusion: To conclude, in this large-scale cohort, we comprehensively depicted the mutational landscape of CSF-ctDNA, explored the biological characteristics of CSF(+) patients, and highlighted the importance of CSF-ctDNA in predicting clinical outcome and CNS relapse in ND-DLBCL patients.

Results: The median target coverage of unique duplex reads across patient ctDNA samples was 717X (interquartile range (IQR): 623-798X), with >88% of targets achieving ≥250X coverage. Somatic variants were detected in 40/56 patients (71.4%), classifying them as ctDNA positive (ctDNA+). Across ctDNA+ cases, 972 somatic variants were identified with a median of 12 variants per patient (IQR: 6-20) and a median variant allele fraction (VAF) of 3%. Stage I cases were significantly associated with ctDNA negativity (8/16 vs. 8/32 in stages II–IV; Fisher’s exact P= 0.047). \n In matching tissue biopsies, somatic variants were detected in 54/56 patients (96.4%) with median 15.5 variants per patient (IQR: 10-27) and median VAF of 23.6% (IQR: 12.7-36.4%). Concordance analysis in 38 ctDNA+ patients with variants detected in paired tissue biopsies a median Jaccard Index of 0.62 (IQR: 0.24-0.76). Results: We identified four distinct mutational signatures: SBS1 and SBS5 both indicative of age, SBS39 of unknown etiology, and SBS84 induced by cytidine deaminase (AID) activity. Unsupervised k-means clustering of mutational signature profiles revealed two distinct molecular subgroups. Classification based on these signatures delineates two distinct subgroups that are reproducible and independently associated with PFS. Overall, incorporating the biological context of mutations could further enhance the prognostic power of ctDNA profiling, enabling earlier and more precise identification of patients at high risk for progressive disease.

pretreatment ctdna-based risk prediction in dlbcl: panel-independent copy-number analysis overcomes inter-assay threshold variability

O 结局指标

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: All SNV-based approaches predicted clinical risk, but absolute ctDNA quantification varied markedly. Even within the same cohort, thresholds defining high-risk disease required separate optimisation for each SNV calling strategy and differed by >10-fold. This variation arose partly from different detection limits for low-allele-fraction variants leading to substantial differences in average mutant allele fraction across different variant calling approaches (matched-germline, unmatched-germline and tumour-only strategies employing different variant calling tools). This variability presents a practical barrier to deploying SNV-based risk stratification across centres, sequencing pipelines and panel designs. \n As an alternative, we derived tumour fraction from genome-wide CNAs. Panel-based sequencing profiles including off-target reads were normalised to cfDNA from 51 healthy individuals. A tumour fraction >0.1 was identified as optimal to define high risk. In univariate analyses, CNA-based stratification strongly predicted TTP (HR 4.97, 95% CI 2.52–9.83, p \n We then assessed technical robustness to variables that typically differ across ctDNA platforms, including genomic regions analysed and reference panel size. Tumour fraction from panel-based sequencing showed strong concordance with low-pass whole-genome sequencing (Pearson’s r >0.9). Tumour fraction remained stable when chromosome arms were iteratively excluded to simulate alternative panel design, suggesting that risk prediction was driven by global tumour-burden signal rather than individual copy number aberrations. Quantification was also stable when at least 20 healthy cfDNA samples were used as reference. Summary/Conclusion: In conclusion, CNA-based estimation of ctDNA tumour fraction provides a technically robust, panel-independent approach to pretreatment risk stratification in LBCL. Application of this computationally simple approach facilitates harmonisation of risk prediction without the requirement for individual centres to standardise sequencing panels and variant calling pipelines.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: VTE occurred in 219/1504 patients (14.6%), with a 1-year cumulative incidence of 3.3% (95% CI 2.4–4.2). Median time to VTE was 72 days, confirming the early clustering of thrombotic events. VTE independently predicts inferior OS (38.5 vs 172.3 months). In univariate analysis, hemoglobin (hb) level, leukocytosis, hypoalbuminemia, body mass index (BMI) > 30, bulky disease, and deep vein compression, were significantly associated with increased VTE risk (p 30 (96.6%), hb level (92.8%), neutrophil count (77.9%), and R-IPI (65.8%), while higher albumin levels showed a consistent protective association (96.1% negative selection). These findings suggest residual multidimensional risk information in our cohort, not fully captured by the composite Model IX weighting. Regarding OS prediction, Model IX again showed superior performance (c-index 0.67, 95% CI 0.65–0.69), outperforming ThroLy, R-IPI, and Khorana. While R-IPI retained strong prognostic value for survival, its discriminatory ability for VTE was limited (see Tab. 1). Conversely, VTE-oriented models, particularly Model IX, captured prognostic information relevant to both thrombotic risk and survival, highlighting a partial biological overlap between disease aggressiveness and thrombotic propensity. Summary/Conclusion: VTE is a frequent early complication in DLBCL and is associated with inferior survival. Model IX showed the best discrimination for VTE and outperformed the other models for OS, supporting its role as the most informative risk stratification tool in this setting. * PC, CGP and IC contributed equally

Results: Between March 2024 and December 2025, 75 patients enrolled, provided 425 samples; 68 completed treatment (study ongoing). The mean age was 63; 44 patients had IPI>3, 10 had prior indolent lymphoma, and 13 experienced disease progression (PD). The mean turnaround time was 18 days, with distant sites (>200 km) requiring 21 days versus 16 days for local sites (p 3 (p Barriers to CART included poor performance status and high disease burden (n=6) and age/frailty (n=4). Mortality was 70% among PD patients. Summary/Conclusion: Real-time ctDNA profiling is feasible, but logistical challenges for clinical implementation remain. There is significant attrition among refractory DLBCL patients eligible for CART in real-world settings. Our panel can identify high-risk patients as early as C2D1, supporting early intervention trials.

O 结局指标

3个月完全缓解率（CR rate）：90%（基于21例可评估患者） 3个月总缓解率（ORR）：95%（基于21例可评估患者） 中位无进展生存期（PFS）：未达到 中位总生存期（OS）：未达到 估计6个月PFS：87.0%（95% CI 68.0-100） 估计6个月OS：95.7%（95% CI 86.7-100） 安全性：细胞因子释放综合征（CRS）发生率74%，主要为1-2级；免疫效应细胞相关神经毒性综合征（ICANS）发生率45.7%，主要为低中度；3-4级血液学毒性：血小板减少20%，中性粒细胞减少17.1%；严重感染5例（14%），其中1例死于感染性休克

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: As of December 31 st 2025 (cut-off), 35 patients underwent leukapheresis and 31 had received axi-cel and were included in the present analysis. Median age was 63 years (range 28–79) and 19 (54%) patients were male. At study entry, 49% had relapsed within 12–24 months and 51% within 24–60 months from first-line CIT; 26% of patients had HBCL double hit, 83% showed Ann Arbor stage III–IV and 74% had an IPI ≥2. \n The CR rate and ORR at 3 months among the 21 patients who had reached this time point at the time of data cutoff were 90% and 95%, respectively. With a median follow-up of 5.9 months (Q1-Q3: 2,4-8.7), the median progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) had not been reached. The estimated 6-month PFS and OS were 87.0% (95% CI 68.0-100) and 95.7% (95% CI 86.7-100), respectively (Figure). \n Regarding safety, a total of 81 adverse events classified as serious adverse events (SAEs) or adverse events of special interest (AESIs) and occurring on or before the cut-off time, were reported. Cytokine release syndrome (CRS) occurred in 74% of patients, predominantly grade 1 (37%) and 2 (28.6%); grade ≥3 CRS was infrequent (8.6%), with no grade 4–5 events. Immune effector cell–associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS) was reported in 45.7% of patients. Most events were low to moderate in severity, with grade 3 and 4 events occurring in 14.6% and 8.3% of patients, respectively; no grade 5 neurotoxicity was observed. Hematologic toxicities were common, with thrombocytopenia (20%) and neutropenia (17.1%) being the most frequently reported grade ≥3 cytopenias. Severe infections were reported in 5 cases (14%), including one patient who died due to a septic shock at 34 days from axi-cel infusion. Summary/Conclusion: In this interim analysis of the LATE-R trial, axi-cel demonstrated remarkably high CR rates in patients with late-relapsing aggressive B-cell lymphomas treated in the second-line setting, with a manageable toxicity profile consistent with the known risks of axi-cel. These findings suggest that patients with late CIT relapses could benefit from axi-cel and support its use in this clinical setting.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: The median age was 66 years (range 17–87), with 70.2% of patients aged ≥60 years. The cohort had high-risk features including: 67.2% had stage IV disease, 65.6% had an IPI score ≥3, 11.5% double/triple-hit biology,15.0% transformed disease and 21.3% were ECOG ≥2. The median CCI was 4 (IQR 3-5).\n \n Efficacy: The overall response rate (ORR) was 93.1%, with a complete response rate (CRR) of 79.1%. Efficacy was consistent across high-risk subgroups. ORR remained high regardless of COO (GCB 92.9% vs. non-GCB 92.5%, p>0.99) or patients with transformations of low-grade lymphoma (96.9% vs. 92.4% de novo, p=0.63). There was no significant difference in CRR between patients with CCI 0.99) or age \n Compliance: 83.3% of patients completed all 6 cycles. For those that did not complete all 6 cycles reasons for stopping early included: adverse events (35.7%), death (25.0%), and progressive disease (23.2%). Cycle 1 dose reductions were significantly more frequent in patients ≥70 years (13.6% vs 5.9%, p=0.011) and those with CCI ≥5 were significantly less likely to complete 6 cycles (76.2% vs 89.6%, p \n Safety: Grade ≥3 infections occurred in 35.8% of patients, with significantly higher rates in those patients ≥70 years (42.4% vs 31.9%, p=0.035). Febrile neutropenia (FN) was reported in 29.6%. Diarrhoea occurred in 48.0% (Grade 3-4: 7.7%). Peripheral neuropathy (PN) was reported in 32.1% (grade 3: 3.0%). Opportunistic infections occurred in 10.8%, including PCP (N=8) and shingles (N=5). \n Summary/Conclusion: In this large real-world UK cohort, Pola-R-CHP demonstrated efficacy and deliverability. The CR rate in this series appears comparable to the trial despite being used in a cohort of patients with high-risk features and a broader range of indications than were included in the POLARIX trial. These data support Pola-R-CHP as a first line standard of care in the real-world setting, however the higher rates of grade ≥3 infections and reduced treatment intensity in patients with advanced age and comorbidities demonstrates a need for vigilant supportive care in this demographic. Survival outcomes will be presented. \n References: \n \n Tilly H, et al. Polatuzumab Vedotin in Previously Untreated Diffuse Large B-Cell Lymphoma. N Engl J Med 2022; 386:351-363. DOI: 10.1056/NEJMoa2115304 \n \n

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Baseline genomic landscape was consistent with prior PCNSL studies, with recurrent mutations in MYD88 (53%), CD79B (47%) and CARD11 (47%). Recurrent copy-number alterations included gains at 3p22.3, 3q29, and 7q21.3 and deletions at 1p13.1, 6p21.32, and 6q21, affecting genes such as BTG2 , CD58 , PRDM1 , and HLA class I/II loci. Whole-genome duplication (WGD) occurred in four tumours and was associated with markedly increased genomic instability. Molecular subtyping assigned 52.6% (10/19) of cases to the DLBclass MYD88/CD79B-driven C5 subtype and 10.5% (2/19) being C2 tumours enriched for TP53 alterations, genomic instability and disruption of MHC class I genes. Concordance between DLBclass and LymphGen classifiers was high. Summary/Conclusion: D isruption of MHC class I - associated genes in diagnostic tumour tissue predicts e POD on BTK i therapy and appears more prognostic than early MRI response. These findings implicate immune evasion as a potential mechanism of resistance to BTK inhibition in rrPCNSL and support the value of genomic profiling of diagnostic tissue to aid response prediction .

O 结局指标

客观缓解率(ORR)：63.2% (12/19) 完全缓解(CR)：3例 未确认完全缓解(unconfirmed CR)：1例 部分缓解(PR)：8例 中位至缓解时间(TTR)：2.2个月 累积持续缓解率：83.3% (95% CI: 51.6–97.9) 中位缓解持续时间(DOR)：未达到 (95%CI下限: 10.1个月) 治疗相关不良事件(TRAEs)：57.9% 常见不良事件：尿路感染21.1%，白细胞减少15.8%，皮疹15.8% 治疗相关严重不良事件：2例（尿路感染1例，脑出血1例）

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: At the data cutoff (September 2025) for the first interim analysis, 19 patients were enrolled. With median follow-up of 10.9 months, tirabrutinib provided promising effectiveness with an ORR of 63.2% (12/19 [complete response in 3, unconfirmed CR in 1, partial response in 8 patients]). The response was characterized by a rapid onset, with a median TTR of 2.2 months. Notably, treatment responses were resilient: among 12 responders, 10 maintained their response during the follow-up period, resulting in a cumulative durable response rate of 83.3% (95% CI: 51.6–97.9). The median DOR has not yet been reached (lower bound 95%CI: 10.1 months). Swimmer plot revealed unique real-world patterns where 9 patients (47.4%) derived continued clinical benefit from ongoing treatment despite initial radiographic assessments of stable disease or initial progression, highlighting that symptomatic stability often guides treatment continuation beyond imaging results. The safety profile was manageable (treatment-emergent AEs 73.7%); common events were urinary tract infection (21.1%), white blood cell count decrease (15.8%), and rash (15.8%). No new safety signals or significant cardiovascular toxicities were observed. Treatment-related AEs (TRAEs) occurred in 57.9% of patients with the majority of onsets occurring within the first 3 months. Treatment-related serious AEs occurred in 2 patients (urinary tract infection in 1 and cerebral haemorrhage in 1 patient). TRAEs were mostly transient; specifically, skin rashes resolved with a median time of 11.5 days. Two Grade 5 events were reported but assessed as unrelated to the treatment. Summary/Conclusion: Tirabrutinib provides rapid and durable treatment responses over a 10.9-month follow-up period in r/r PCNSL patients. These results, along with high cumulative durability and a consistent safety profile, support its role as a key targeted therapy in real-world clinical practice in Taiwan.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Twenty patients were enrolled between February 2023 and December 2024. The median age was 75 years (range, 48–81), and all patients had DLBCL, not otherwise specified (DLBCL-NOS) with secondary CNS involvement. Central pathological review classified 9 patients as the germinal center B-cell–like (GCB) subtype, 10 as the non-GCB subtype, and 1 patient as unclassifiable. Three patients had cerebrospinal fluid disease, including one without parenchymal lesions. The median number of prior therapies was 3.5 (range, 1–8). Eighteen patients were evaluable for efficacy by ICR. The ORR was 66.7% (95% CI, 41.0–86.7; p Summary/Conclusion: Tirabrutinib demonstrated clinically meaningful activity with a manageable safety profile in heavily pretreated patients with R/R SCNSL. The phase II CRYSTAL/NCCH2201 study supports tirabrutinib as a promising therapeutic option for this disease with extremely poor prognosis.

106DLBCL/LBCL回顾性/真实世界研究LBCL/HGBLCAR-T/细胞治疗S283

综合多组分分析确定了与大b细胞淋巴瘤car-t治疗后不同结果相关的基因组亚型

integrated multi-omic profiling identifies genomic subtypes associated with differential outcomes after car-t therapy in large b-cell lymphoma

P 患者群体

大B细胞淋巴瘤；N=112

I 干预措施

试验药/方案：阿基仑赛；Lisocabtagene maraleucel；Tisagenlecleucel；靶点：CD19；类别：CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，逆转录病毒载体RV，经基因修饰；CAR-T，外周血，自体细胞，慢病毒载体LV，经基因修饰

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

1. BN2亚型 vs 其他亚型：PFS 16% (95% CI 6-46, p=0.017)，PFS6显著更低(p=0.009)，CR率显著更低(p=0.041) 2. 多变量Cox回归：BN2与较差的PFS和PFS6独立相关(均p<0.05) 3. 炎症TME亚型：1年PFS 19% (95% CI 7-52) 4. DHIT阳性 vs DHIT阴性：1年PFS 46% vs 31%（数值上有利） 5. GCB亚组中，DZsig阳性与阴性PFS相似（因样本量小未正式检验）

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: Among 112 patients with available molecular data, median follow-up was 66 months (IQR 46-73). CAR-T products included axicabtagene ciloleucel (49%), tisagenlecleucel (38%), and lisocabtagene maraleucel (13%). Fifty-four percent of tumors were germinal center B-cell type, 46% activated B-cell type, and 17% were DHIT-positive. \n WES data were available in 99 patients. BostonGene’s Lymphly classifier assigned genomic subtypes to a larger proportion of evaluable cases compared with LymphGen and demonstrated improved outcome discrimination ( Fig. 1A ). Inferior outcomes were primarily driven by the BN2 subtype, which was associated with worse PFS (16%, 95% CI 6-46, p=0.017), lower PFS6 (p=0.009), and reduced CR rates (p=0.041) compared with other evaluable subgroups ( Fig. 1B ). In multivariable Cox models adjusting for relevant clinical covariates, BN2 remained independently associated with inferior PFS and PFS6 (both p \n RNA-seq data were available for 55 patients. RNA-defined TME subtypes and DHIT status were not significantly associated with PFS in univariable analyses. The inflammatory TME subtype demonstrated numerically inferior outcomes, with a 1-year PFS of 19% (95% CI 7-52) compared with 36% and 41% in the mesenchymal and depleted subtypes, respectively, whereas DHIT-positive cases showed numerically favorable 1-year PFS (46% vs 31%) ( Fig. 1C ). Within the GCB subgroup, the Dzsig showed similar PFS between DZsig-positive and DZsig-negative cases ( Fig 1D ); formal statistical testing was not performed due to limited sample size. Summary/Conclusion: Multi-omic profiling identifies biologically defined high-risk subgroups after CAR-T therapy, highlighting BN2 as a genomically driven resistance phenotype. Genomic classification may refine patient selection and enable mechanism-based therapeutic strategies in LBCL.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: In total 5298 pts were included: 5066 DLBCL-NOS, 177 HGBL-MYC/BCL2, and 55 HGBL-NOS. Median age was 62.6 years (y) and did not differ between groups (p=0.51). Median time from diagnosis to CAR T was shorter in both HGBL cohorts (10.4 months (mo) for MYC/BCL2; 10.9 mo for NOS) compared with DLBCL-NOS (15.3 mo; p Summary/Conclusion: In this large EBMT RW cohort, pts with HGBL-NOS and HGBL-MYC/BCL2 achieved promising PFS, despite a high-risk clinical profile at infusion. The results indicate that CD19 CAR T cell therapy may mitigate the adverse biology of HGBL in the R/R setting. Despite its limitations, including the retrospective design, absence of central pathology review, and potential under-reporting of MYC/BCL2-rearranged cases, these findings provide contemporary, entity-specific benchmarks and support CD19 CAR T as a very relevant therapeutic option for R/R HGBL, informing treatment sequencing and future study design.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 561 patients with DLBCL were enrolled, including 123 treated with BsAbs and 438 treated with CAR T-cell therapies. The mean age at the index event (initiation of BsAbs for Cohort 1; initiation of CAR T-cell therapy for Cohort 2) was 47.2±9.2 for Cohort 1 and 44.5±11.3 for Cohort 2 (p=0.015). There were 63% and 66% male patients, respectively (p=0.664). Over a 2-year follow-up period from the index event, Cohort 1 had a significantly higher risk of death compared to Cohort 2 (RR 1.468, 95%CI 1.116-1.932). Cohort 1 had a significantly shorter two-year OS probability and a higher risk of death at two years (47.5% vs. 67.3% survival probability at 2 years from the index event, log-rank test, χ2=20.034, p Summary/Conclusion: In this real-world analysis of DLBCL patients ≤60 years old, treatment with BsAbs was linked to worse OS and higher death risk compared to CAR T-cell therapies. These findings remained consistent before and after PSM, highlighting the robustness of the results. While CAR T-cell therapies showed better survival over 2 years, the data's aggregate nature limits detailed clinical interpretation, including disease and treatment factors affecting outcomes. Still, the results support using CAR T-cell therapies over BsAbs for eligible younger patients with R/R DLBCL and emphasize the need for more research with patient-level data to improve comparative assessments.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 273 patients were included, with 161 receiving liso-cel and 112 receiving BsAb (median [IQR] age at index, 72 y [62–77] vs 75 y [65–81]; DLBCL, not otherwise specified, 87% vs 76%; high-grade B-cell lymphoma, 2% vs 8%; elevated LDH, 28% vs 54%; bulky disease, 66% vs 66%; 3L, 70% vs 54%; and median follow-up time of 12.4 mo vs 9.1 mo). In both unadjusted and adjusted analyses, liso-cel was associated with a statistically significant improvement in OS (adjusted HR, 0.62; P =0.023) and PFS (adjusted HR, 0.53; P P =0.004) and CRR (61% vs 28%; P Table 1 ). \n In a sensitivity analysis of 3L-only patients (liso-cel, n=113; BsAb, n=60), liso-cel had a statistically significant benefit for OS (HR, 0.35; P P with higher ORR (83% vs 64%) and CRR (65% vs 27%) vs BsAb. \n Any-grade cytokine release syndrome (CRS) and immune effector cell–associated neurotoxicity syndrome (ICANS) incidence was higher with liso-cel, mostly due to grade 1–2 events ( Table 2 ). There was no grade ≥3 CRS with liso-cel and low rates of grade ≥3 ICANS overall. Rates of prolonged cytopenia (liso-cel, 32%; BsAb, 29%) and infections (liso-cel, 8%; BsAb, 14%) were comparable between cohorts. There were lower hospitalization and ICU admission rates with liso-cel vs BsAb across most time periods ( Figure 1 ). Summary/Conclusion: In this retrospective, RW analysis, liso-cel demonstrated significantly better efficacy and similar HCRU and safety vs BsAb as a 3L+ therapy for LBCL; further data are needed to compare these treatments in earlier lines of therapy. Summary/Conclusion: RAG-enhanced LLMs achieved 83% acceptability in R/R DLBCL recommendations, comparable to their performance on health benchmarks. EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: The distribution by deprivation was: 58 Low (28.9%), 102 Medium (50.7%), and 41 High (20.4%). The distribution by ethnicity was: 166 White (89.2%), 15 Asian (8.1%), 5 Black (2.7%) (18 Unknown). There was a trend to greater proportion of ethnic minority patients from more deprived areas (Low 7.3%, Medium 10.6%, High 17.5%, p=0.14). Patients from the most deprived areas travelled less for CAR-T (median distance by IMD: Low 42.6km, Medium 43.1km, High 29.6km, p=0.026), likely reflecting the inner-city location of most centres. 8% of patients travelled >100km. \n There were no significant differences in baseline characteristics (including age, stage, LDH, bulk, IPI) according to deprivation. 94.7% of patients received bridging therapy, with no significant differences by deprivation. Importantly, there were no differences in vein-to-vein time, or drop-out rate by deprivation (92.0% infused for whole cohort). \n In the low deprivation group, there was a trend to superior response to bridging (overall response rate by IMD: Low 68.0%, Medium 43.1%, High 44.1%, p=0.099), and more grade 3+ CRS events (% by IMD: Low 9.4%, Medium 3.2%, High 0%, p=0.024); but no significant difference in grade 3+ ICANS, tocilizumab/steroid use or ICU admission. There were no significant differences in complete metabolic response rate, PFS/OS, or non-relapse mortality by deprivation. There were no significant differences in toxicity / efficacy outcomes in ethnic minority patients, or for patients travelling >100km. There were no reported COVID-19 deaths in this cohort, highlighting the evolution in COVID-19 risk. \n \n Summary/Conclusion: Our data suggest similar outcomes for patients receiving 2L axi-cel irrespective of socio-economic deprivation, ethnicity or distance to centre in a diverse UK cohort, contrasting with findings at 3L. Moving CAR-T to earlier treatment line, more pro-active bridging strategies, and the decline in the COVID-19 pandemic, may have helped mitigate competing risks felt by more deprived patients; although deprivation, ethnicity and distance may impact on patient experience and outcomes in ways not captured here. Furthermore, the effect of these factors on rate of referral for CAR-T was not examined and warrants separate analysis. We saw fewer patients travelling >100km - attributable to an increase in the number of UK CAR-T centres - but for those still facing this barrier, outcomes were equivalent, underlining that they should still be offered CAR-T and the necessary support to travel.

Results: A total of N=413 patients were included (2L n=184, ≥3L n=229). Baseline characteristics are summarized in Table 1. Briefly, the 2L cohort showed a better ECOG performance status at infusion, lower R-IPI, lower prior ASCT exposure, lower rates of bulky disease and elevated LDH, and more frequent use of bridging therapy. No differences were observed in the median time from apheresis to infusion between groups. Comparing 2L vs ≥3L, any-grade CRS occurred in 95% vs 92%, with grade ≥3 CRS in 4% vs 8% (p=0.002). Median time-to-onset was 2 days in both groups and median duration 4 vs 5 days (p=0.02). Tocilizumab was administered in 61% vs 62% patients (median doses 1.5 vs 2, p=0.03), and corticosteroids were administered in 48% vs 32% (p ICU admission related to toxicity occurred in 21% vs 24%. No differences were observed in non-relapse mortality (NRM). Summary/Conclusion: In this real-world DLBCL axi-cel cohort, second line of therapy was associated with lower rates of grade ≥3 early toxicities (CRS and ICANS) as compared to ≥3L. Despite this reduced incidence of high-grade toxicity, corticosteroid use for CRS was more frequent in the 2L cohort, likely reflecting a temporal shift toward earlier and more proactive toxicity management in the more recent treatment period. Further analysis are needed to discard an impact of disease characteristics on these findings.

Results: The median age was 67 years; 92.3% were in stage III–IV and 86.2% had bone marrow involvement. The ED rate was 19.2%. The enrichment of the MCD subtype suggests that integrating targeted agents, such as BTK inhibitors, warrants further investigation.

O 结局指标

2年OS：标准组80%（75%,86%），改良组83%（76%,92%），p=0.90 2年DFS：标准组77%（72%,83%），改良组78%（69%,88%），p=0.79 5年OS：标准组72%（65%,79%），改良组72%（62%,84%） 5年DFS：标准组68%（61%,75%），改良组67%（56%,79%）

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 294 patients were included. Among these, 210 patients (71%) with a median age of 68 years (range 19-84) continued full-dose vincristine throughout the R-CHOP-therapy, while 84 patients (29%) with a median age of 67 years (range 19-84) transitioned to modified treatment. Baseline demographics and disease characteristics were largely comparable between groups. In both groups, the majority were male (58%) and had performance status 0-1 (88%). Extra nodal disease was present in 60% and 62% of cases, respectively, and low-intermediate risk disease (IPI 0-2) in 56% and 54%. In the modified cohort, 14 (17%) underwent vincristine dose reduction, 10 (12%) had vincristine omitted, 38 (45%) received vinblastine substitution, and 22 (26%) experienced both reduction and substitution. \n The landmark analysis showed no statistically significant difference in adjusted OS (p=0.90) or DFS (p=0.79). The two years OS estimates were 80% (75%, 86%) and 83% (76%, 92%) between patients remaining on R‑CHOP and those who received modified vincristine treatment, respectively (Figure 1). The corresponding two years DFS estimates were 77% (72%, 83%) and 78% (69, 88%). The five years OS estimates were 72% (65%,79%) and 72% (62%,84%) and the five years DFS estimates were 68% (61%,75%) and 67% (56%,79%). Both curves demonstrated a gradual decline over 10 years without clear separation between treatment strategies. Summary/Conclusion: In this population‑based cohort of patients with de novo DLBCL, modification of vincristine during R‑CHOP therapy either through dose reduction, omission, or substitution with vinblastine, no significant differences in overall survival or disease‑free survival compared with continued standard full-dose vincristine throughout the R‑CHOP-therapy were found. These findings suggest that adjustments of vincristine doses can be implemented without compromising long‑term clinical outcomes.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 202 patients were included, with a median age of 55 years (range from 18 to 81). 96 (47.5%) patients received consolidative RT after chemotherapy , while 106 (52.5%) received CT alone. R-CHOP-like regimens were used in 83.2% of cases, with 48% and 48% completing baseline and post-treatment PET/CT assessments, respectively. With a median follow-up of 80.8 months, the 5-year OS, PFS, and LRC rates were 98.5% , 92.2% and 97.6% in the CT+RT group , compared to 86.4% (P=0.06), 83.5(P=0.04)and 95.8% (P=0.5) for the CT-alone group, respectively. Although a statistical difference in PFS was observed, consolidative RT did not significantly improve OS or LRC, consistent with the exceptionally low local recurrence rate (only 6 cases) across the entire cohort. A total of 14 deaths were recorded during follow-up. Notably, only 3 patients (21.4%) died of lymphoma-specific causes, 11 patients (78.6%) died of non-lymphoma-related causes, including second primary malignancies (n=3), hepatic disease (n=1), and other unknown causes (n=7). Survival outcomes were favorable and equivalent to the age- and sex-matched general population in both groups, with SMR of 0.64 (95% CI: 0.17–1.64; P = 0.54) for the CT+RT group and 1.41 (95% CI: 0.68–2.60; P = 0.25) for the CT-alone group, indicating that patients achieved life expectancy comparable to the general population. Competing risk analysis revealed that NLM was a prominent contributor to late mortality events, whereas the cumulative incidence of LSM remained low and comparable between the CT-alone and CT+RT groups (2.3% vs 1.6%, p = 0.53). Summary/Conclusion: For limited-stage PG-DLBCL achieving CR after first-line chemotherapy, consolidative RT provides limited survival benefit due to exceptional local control and survival normalization. Competing risk analysis identifies NLM as the primary late mortality driver. While RT may not be mandatory for all, it may serve as a strategic enabler for chemotherapy de-escalation. The next step is to further investigate whether RT can serve as a key enabler for chemotherapy de-escalation.

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: 494 pts were included; 68% (n=338) with LBCL/HGBCL (25% transformed), 19% FL (n=94), 13% other histologies (n=62). Pts received glofit (41%), epco (35%), or mosu (24%). Prior to BsAb, median age was 69 yrs (range 22-93) and 64% had stage 4 disease. The median pre-treatment (tx) WBC was 5.4 (range 0.1-205), ANC was 3.5 (range 0-82), ALC was 0.70 (range 0-197), and NLR was 10 (range 0-274). There was no difference among age, sex, stage, elevated LDH, or prior therapies (CAR-T, auto-SCT, number of prior lines of therapy) among pts with pre-tx high NLR vs low NLR. Use of BsAb was similar other than lower use of mosu among pts with high NLR vs low NLR (13% vs 31%). At a median follow up of 13 months, the median PFS and OS among all pts were 6.2 months and 21.5 months, respectively. The optimal cutoff for a high NLR was determined to be 5.0 for PFS and 5.3 for OS. For high vs low NLR, the median PFS and OS were 3.8 vs 12.1 months and 8.8 vs 21.5 months, respectively. After adjusting for baseline clinico-pathological variables, high NLR was independently associated with an inferior PFS (NLR>5.0, HR 1.45, 95% CI 1.1-1.8, p 5.3, HR 1.4, 95% CI 1.06-2.05, p=0.02) compared to low NLR (Figure 1). NLR as a continuous variable was also significantly associated with PFS (p=0.02) and OS (p Summary/Conclusion: A high pre-tx NLR (>5.0) is associated with inferior PFS and OS in pts treated with BsAbs, independent of disease subtype or specific agent. NLR is a readily available prognostic marker of response and survival, unlike more complex assays of T-cell phenotype and function. Further investigation into the immunobiological mechanisms driving BsAb resistance in non-responders is warranted.

Results: \n Median age of the cohort was 67 years. CH was detected in the granulocyte compartment in 37.7% of patients, with DNMT3A (20.5%) and TET2 (14.6%) as the most frequently mutated genes (Fig. 1A). Among CH + patients, DNMT3A mutations were significantly enriched in the C3 molecular subtype of DLBCL ( p =0.005) (Fig. 1B). Both DNMT3A and TET2 mutations significantly associated with an increased risk of second primary malignancies (5-year CIF: 7.1 vs 16.3, P =0.03; 7.3 vs 19.4, p . In plasma, cfDNA sequencing detected 78 of 80 CH granulocyte mutations (97.5% sensitivity), with strong VAF correlation between compartments (r=0.89, p The most common mutations were DNMT3A (22.4%) and TET2 (15.0%). In PB, CH + patients demonstrated marginally reduced PFS (55.8% vs. 64.1%) and OS (69.8% vs. 72.4%) relative to CH - cases, without however reaching statistical significance ( p =0.547 and P =0.466, respectively). At EOT, the prevalence of CH increased from 34.7% at baseline to 50.5% ( p p mutations of PPM1D were mostly undetectable before treatment but emerged following chemoimmunotherapy (CIT), increasing from 1.1% baseline cases to 16.3% EOT cases and showing the highest inferred clonal fitness (Fig. 1D). All PPM1D mutations were already detectable after C3, with higher clonal fitness from baseline to C3 compared to C3 to EOT, suggesting an early CIT-driven bottleneck effect ( p =0.03). In tissue biopsies, at least one TI-CH mutation occurred in 42.9% of patients, most commonly involving DNMT3A (21.4%, VAF range 0.4–27.0) and TET2 (16.1%, VAF range 0.4–27.4), almost mutually exclusive. At a median follow-up of 69 months, TI- DNMT3A + patients had a significantly inferior PFS (33.3% vs 70.9%, p =0.009) and OS (41.7% vs 83.7%, p DNMT3A − cases. This adverse impact remained significant after adjusting for the international prognostic index (Fig. 1E). \n Summary/Conclusion: \n Multi-compartment profiling shows that CH in DLBCL is frequent and detectable in multiple compartments, enriched in specific molecular subtypes, and associated with an increased risk of second primary malignancies. R-CHOP–based therapy promotes expansion of CH clones, including early emergence of PPM1D mutations. While CH in PB did not significantly affect survival, TI-CH DNMT3A mutations emerged as an independent predictor of inferior PFS and OS in DLBCL treated with CIT.

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：a disease specific prognostic score for immunodeficiency-associated primary cns lymphoma: an international primary cns lymphoma collaborative group (ipcg) study

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: A total of 308 patients with ID-PCNSL were identified. Underlying immunodeficiency resulted from immunosuppressive therapy for organ transplantation (41.2%) or autoimmune disease (36.7%), and from HIV infection (21.7%). All tumors were classified as diffuse large B-cell lymphomas, with Epstein–Barr virus (EBV) detected in 79.2%. \n Most patients (91.4%) received curative-intent induction therapy, predominantly systemic chemotherapy (97.5%), while radiation alone was uncommon (2.1%). Rituximab–methotrexate (RM)–based regimens were most frequently used (69.8%), followed by rituximab-based (15.6%) and methotrexate-based therapy alone (12.7%). Best overall response rate (ORR) to first-line therapy was 77% (complete response 50%; partial response 27%). RM-based chemotherapy achieved higher ORR (85%) compared with rituximab-based (68%, p=0.01) or methotrexate-based regimens alone (52%, p \n Outcomes were heterogeneous, with a median overall survival (OS) of 54 months ( Fig. 1A) . Multivariable analysis identified increasing age (HR 1.05 per year, 95% CI 1.02–1.07; p Fig. 1B ), Karnofsky Performance Status (KPS) Fig. 1C ), and EBV positivity (HR 3.26, 95% CI 1.47–7.33; p=0.004; Fig. 1D ) as independent predictors of inferior OS. A prognostic score incorporating these factors (age >60 years, KPS Fig. 1E ) stratified patients into three risk groups with median OS of 135, 29, and 3 months for patients with ≤1, 2, and 3 risk factors, respectively (p Fig. 1F ). The score retained prognostic significance in patients treated with RM-based regimens. Compared with MSKCC and IELSG scores, the new model demonstrated improved performance with lower AIC and higher concordance index and time-dependent AUC. Summary/Conclusion: This large international cohort defines the clinical spectrum of ID-PCNSL and demonstrates substantial heterogeneity in outcomes. Immune reconstitution combined with RM-based therapy is associated with high response rates across immunodeficiency subtypes. A simple prognostic score based on age, performance status, and EBV status provides robust risk stratification, remains informative in RM-treated patients, and outperforms established models developed for immunocompetent PCNSL.

原发性中枢神经系统淋巴瘤临床病理预后模型的建立与验证

development and validation of a clinicopathological prognostic model for primary central nervous system lymphoma

P 患者群体

中枢神经系统淋巴瘤；N=180；疾病阶段：原发性

I 干预措施

回顾性临床研究结果：development and validation of a clinicopathological prognostic model for primary central nervous system lymphoma

C 对照措施

未明确对照；按单臂、观察性、真实世界、基础研究或原表未提取处理

O 结局指标

中位年龄60岁（18-82岁）；男性占56.67%；DLBCL病理亚型占95%；多变量Cox回归显示年龄≥60岁（HR:2.58），ECOG-PS≥2（HR:4.28），MYC表达（HR:2.76）为独立预后因素；模型在训练集和验证集的AUC分别为0.74和0.89

EHA原文结果（中文字段未通过数字核对）

Results: The median age at diagnosis of the enrolled 180 patients was 60 years (range: 18–82 years), with 56.67% (102/180) being male. Diffuse large B-cell lymphoma (DLBCL) constituted the predominant pathological subtype (95%, 171/180). Treatment modalities included subtotal/total tumor resection in 135 cases (75%), biopsy alone in 45 cases (25%), high-dose methotrexate (HD-MTX)-based chemotherapy in 67 cases (37.22%), and combination therapies (including radiotherapy or hematopoietic cell transplantation) in 30 cases (16.7%). Multivariable Cox regression identified age ≥ 60 years (HR: 2.58, p 2 (HR: 4.28, p p (Figure 1A) . The model exhibited good discrimination, with area under the curve values of 0.74 and 0.89 in the training and validation cohorts, respectively (Figure 1B-C) . Calibration curves demonstrated high consistency between the predicted probabilities and actual observations. Furthermore, risk stratification based on this model revealed significant differences in survival status among patients in different risk groups, indicating that this risk stratification strategy can effectively differentiate patient prognosis (Figure 1D-E) . Summary/Conclusion: This study presents a novel prognostic model integrating age, ECOG-PS, and MYC expression to predict OS in newly diagnosed PCNSL patients. By incorporating high-risk clinicopathological features associated with tumor aggressiveness, this model may facilitate more individualized treatment planning.
